\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+I\+NG}{ARP\_QUEUEING}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+I\+NG~0}

A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+I\+NG==1\+: Multiple outgoing packets are queued during hardware address resolution. By default, only the most recent packet is queued per IP address. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} is sufficient for most protocols and mainly reduces T\+CP connection startup time. Set this to 1 if you know your application sends more than one packet in a row to an IP address that is not in the A\+RP cache. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a924936a814564dbdb0bc950d255a83b9}\label{opt_8h_a924936a814564dbdb0bc950d255a83b9}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+ST}{DNS\_LOCAL\_HOSTLIST}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+ST~0}

D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+ST\+: Implements a local host-\/to-\/address list. If enabled, you have to define \hyperlink{structdefine}{define} D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+IT \{\{\char`\"{}host1\char`\"{}, 0x123\}, \{\char`\"{}host2\char`\"{}, 0x234\}\} (an array of structs name/address, where address is an u32\+\_\+t in network byte order).

Instead, you can also use an external function\+: \hyperlink{structdefine}{define} D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+K\+U\+P\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+R\+N(x) extern u32\+\_\+t my\+\_\+lookup\+\_\+function(const char $\ast$name) that returns the IP address or I\+N\+A\+D\+D\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE if not found. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a8235a5fb0a1c1cceeee670cf95612ba8}\label{opt_8h_a8235a5fb0a1c1cceeee670cf95612ba8}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC@{D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC}}
\index{D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC@{D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC}{DNS\_LOCAL\_HOSTLIST\_IS\_DYNAMIC}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} D\+N\+S\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+H\+O\+S\+T\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC~0}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+A\+D\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE}{ETH\_PAD\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+A\+D\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE~0}

E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+A\+D\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE\+: number of bytes added before the ethernet header to ensure alignment of payload after that header. Since the header is 14 bytes long, without this padding e.\+g. addresses in the IP header will not be aligned on a 32-\/bit boundary, so setting this to 2 can speed up 32-\/bit-\/platforms. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_abff5d1e0b334f5b45bd2b8bbb675411e}\label{opt_8h_abff5d1e0b334f5b45bd2b8bbb675411e}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+I\+ES~0}

E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+I\+ES==1\+: enable code to support static A\+RP table entries (using etharp\+\_\+add\+\_\+static\+\_\+entry/etharp\+\_\+remove\+\_\+static\+\_\+entry). \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a70ce0ecf56cf5fab000134e66d863f90}\label{opt_8h_a70ce0ecf56cf5fab000134e66d863f90}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN@{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN}}
\index{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN@{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN}{ETHARP\_SUPPORT\_VLAN}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN~0}

E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+V\+L\+AN==1\+: support receiving ethernet packets with V\+L\+AN header. Additionally, you can define E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+V\+L\+A\+N\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK to an u16\+\_\+t V\+L\+AN ID to check. If E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+V\+L\+A\+N\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK is defined, only V\+L\+A\+N-\/traffic for this V\+L\+AN is accepted. If E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+V\+L\+A\+N\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK is not defined, all traffic is accepted. Alternatively, define a function/define E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+V\+L\+A\+N\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+\_\+\+F\+N(eth\+\_\+hdr, vlan) that returns 1 to accept a packet or 0 to drop a packet. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a5348b198e7e7b447cbe714913895e924}\label{opt_8h_a5348b198e7e7b447cbe714913895e924}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC@{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC}}
\index{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC@{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC}{ETHARP\_TRUST\_IP\_MAC}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC~0}

E\+T\+H\+A\+R\+P\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+S\+T\+\_\+\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AC==1\+: Incoming IP packets cause the A\+RP table to be updated with the source M\+AC and IP addresses supplied in the packet. You may want to disable this if you do not trust L\+AN peers to have the correct addresses, or as a limited approach to attempt to handle spoofing. If disabled, lw\+IP will need to make a new A\+RP request if the peer is not already in the A\+RP table, adding a little latency. The peer {\itshape is} in the A\+RP table if it requested our address before. Also notice that this slows down input processing of every IP packet! \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9595904a1cb9bfe0b9b1d958abdc923a}\label{opt_8h_a9595904a1cb9bfe0b9b1d958abdc923a}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+RD}{IP\_FORWARD}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+RD~0}

I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+RD==1\+: Enables the ability to forward IP packets across network interfaces. If you are going to run lw\+IP on a device with only one network interface, define this to 0. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9e761df07c4e93901858741d4771dbc7}\label{opt_8h_a9e761df07c4e93901858741d4771dbc7}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF@{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF@{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF}{IP\_FORWARD\_ALLOW\_TX\_ON\_RX\_NETIF}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF~0}

I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+W\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+X\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+IF==1\+: allow ip\+\_\+forward() to send packets back out on the netif where it was received. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} should only be used for wireless networks. A\+T\+T\+E\+N\+T\+I\+ON\+: When this is 1, make sure your netif driver correctly marks incoming link-\/layer-\/broadcast/multicast packets as such using the corresponding pbuf flags! \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_af85c8bdd5035b6cada790b4cc2a209a4}\label{opt_8h_af85c8bdd5035b6cada790b4cc2a209a4}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG@{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG@{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG}{IP\_FRAG}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG~1}

I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG==1\+: Fragment outgoing IP packets if their size exceeds M\+TU. Note that this option does not affect incoming packet sizes, which can be controlled via I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_acf9edad9d50d86009044946e6db38c01}\label{opt_8h_acf9edad9d50d86009044946e6db38c01}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF@{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF@{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF}{IP\_FRAG\_USES\_STATIC\_BUF}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF~0}

I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF==1\+: Use a static M\+T\+U-\/sized buffer for IP fragmentation. Otherwise pbufs are allocated and reference the original packet data to be fragmented (or with L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+B\+UF==1, new P\+B\+U\+F\+\_\+\+R\+AM pbufs are used for fragments). A\+T\+T\+E\+N\+T\+I\+ON\+: I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+UF==1 may not be used for D\+M\+A-\/enabled M\+A\+Cs! \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_aa956b0167c37a2265b55e2d0204a3933}\label{opt_8h_aa956b0167c37a2265b55e2d0204a3933}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED@{I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED@{I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED}{IP\_OPTIONS\_ALLOWED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED~1}

I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED\+: Defines the behavior for IP options. I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED==0\+: All packets with IP options are dropped. I\+P\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+S\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+ED==1\+: IP options are allowed (but not parsed). \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a4cdc3e9a4a1c01d1f7f0e723a1b2ec33}\label{opt_8h_a4cdc3e9a4a1c01d1f7f0e723a1b2ec33}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG}{IP\_REASS\_DEBUG}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG~L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+O\+FF}

I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG\+: Enable debugging in \hyperlink{ip__frag_8c}{ip\+\_\+frag.\+c} for both frag \& reass. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a29084a46d7d4be30e8029d356bca0394}\label{opt_8h_a29084a46d7d4be30e8029d356bca0394}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS@{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS@{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS}{IP\_REASS\_MAX\_PBUFS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS~10}

I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS\+: Total maximum amount of pbufs waiting to be reassembled. Since the received pbufs are enqueued, be sure to configure P\+B\+U\+F\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE $>$ I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+P\+B\+U\+FS so that the stack is still able to receive packets even if the maximum amount of fragments is enqueued for reassembly! \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ad41122bd0b5485a18a4415c8f953727b}\label{opt_8h_ad41122bd0b5485a18a4415c8f953727b}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE@{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE@{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE}{IP\_REASS\_MAXAGE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE~3}

I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+A\+GE\+: Maximum time (in multiples of I\+P\+\_\+\+T\+M\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL -\/ so seconds, normally) a fragmented IP packet waits for all fragments to arrive. If not all fragments arrived in this time, the whole packet is discarded. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a1a31ab0e0f37b17d40fa7c35bc2c4f69}\label{opt_8h_a1a31ab0e0f37b17d40fa7c35bc2c4f69}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY@{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY@{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY}{IP\_REASSEMBLY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY~1}

I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY==1\+: Reassemble incoming fragmented IP packets. Note that this option does not affect outgoing packet sizes, which can be controlled via I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a0b2c993fd940f5774108298933310384}\label{opt_8h_a0b2c993fd940f5774108298933310384}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST@{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST@{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST}{IP\_SOF\_BROADCAST}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST~0}

I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST=1\+: Use the S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST field to enable broadcast filter per pcb on udp and raw send operations. To enable broadcast filter on recv operations, you also have to set I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV=1. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a0f1fbf42d3344bf87cd056d48ddca3db}\label{opt_8h_a0f1fbf42d3344bf87cd056d48ddca3db}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV@{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV}}
\index{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV@{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV}{IP\_SOF\_BROADCAST\_RECV}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV~0}

I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+CV (requires I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+O\+F\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST=1) enable the broadcast filter on recv operations. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_af50575a4895e26ea2c01d1f2269487be}\label{opt_8h_af50575a4895e26ea2c01d1f2269487be}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS}{IP\_STATS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS~1}

I\+P\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS==1\+: Enable IP stats. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ac9a4fbb46df3c0f479a334d0e34fb74f}\label{opt_8h_ac9a4fbb46df3c0f479a334d0e34fb74f}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS@{I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS}}
\index{I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS@{I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS}{IPFRAG\_STATS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS~(\hyperlink{opt_8h_a1a31ab0e0f37b17d40fa7c35bc2c4f69}{I\+P\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+S\+E\+M\+B\+LY} $\vert$$\vert$ \hyperlink{opt_8h_af85c8bdd5035b6cada790b4cc2a209a4}{I\+P\+\_\+\+F\+R\+AG})}

I\+P\+F\+R\+A\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS==1\+: Enable IP fragmentation stats. Default is on if using either frag or reass. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ae58b452782d0327ae728192686c5a84a}\label{opt_8h_ae58b452782d0327ae728192686c5a84a}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS}{LINK\_STATS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS~1}

L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TS==1\+: Enable link stats. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a0a3ef6098813c103e5aba07da76e15e2}\label{opt_8h_a0a3ef6098813c103e5aba07da76e15e2}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+XT@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+XT}}
\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+XT@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+XT}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+XT}{LWIP\_ALLOW\_MEM\_FREE\_FROM\_OTHER\_CONTEXT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+F\+R\+O\+M\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+XT~0}

Set this to 1 if you want to free P\+B\+U\+F\+\_\+\+R\+AM pbufs (or call \hyperlink{sdk_2lib_2drivers_2lwip_2src_2core_2mem_8c_a65169147c44e9db60d997819af9b455c}{mem\+\_\+free()}) from interrupt context (or another context that doesn\textquotesingle{}t allow waiting for a semaphore). If set to 1, mem\+\_\+malloc will be protected by a semaphore and S\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+E\+CT, while mem\+\_\+free will only use S\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+E\+CT. mem\+\_\+malloc S\+Y\+S\+\_\+\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+U\+N\+P\+R\+O\+T\+E\+C\+Ts with each loop so that mem\+\_\+free can run.

A\+T\+T\+E\+N\+T\+I\+ON\+: As you can see from the above description, this leads to dis-\// enabling interrupts often, which can be slow! Also, on low memory, mem\+\_\+malloc can need longer.

If you don\textquotesingle{}t want that, at least for N\+O\+\_\+\+S\+YS=0, you can still use the following functions to enqueue a deallocation call which then runs in the tcpip\+\_\+thread context\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item pbuf\+\_\+free\+\_\+callback(p);
\item mem\+\_\+free\+\_\+callback(m); 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9609a014bba4638cc191d6a8f9556c87}\label{opt_8h_a9609a014bba4638cc191d6a8f9556c87}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+RP@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+RP}}
\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+RP@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+A\+RP}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}

\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+I\+NG@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+I\+NG}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+I\+NG~0}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+I\+NG==1\+: respond to broadcast pings (default is unicast only) \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9f60183f0442bdbeefd6b395c6647613}\label{opt_8h_a9f60183f0442bdbeefd6b395c6647613}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+O\+PY@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+O\+PY}}
\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+O\+PY@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+O\+PY}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+O\+PY}{LWIP\_CHECKSUM\_ON\_COPY}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL}{LWIP\_DBG\_MIN\_LEVEL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL~L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+A\+LL}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+H\+O\+O\+K\+\_\+\+I\+P4\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T(pbuf, input\+\_\+netif)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item called from \hyperlink{lwip_2src_2core_2ipv4_2ip_8c_a3c420dab0c6760df099a2d688fa42a26}{ip\+\_\+input()} (I\+Pv4)
\item pbuf\+: received struct pbuf passed to \hyperlink{lwip_2src_2core_2ipv4_2ip_8c_a3c420dab0c6760df099a2d688fa42a26}{ip\+\_\+input()}
\item input\+\_\+netif\+: struct netif on which the packet has been received Return values\+:
\item 0\+: Hook has not consumed the packet, packet is processed as normal
\item != 0\+: Hook has consumed the packet. If the hook consumed the packet, \textquotesingle{}pbuf\textquotesingle{} is in the responsibility of the hook (i.\+e. free it when done). L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+H\+O\+O\+K\+\_\+\+I\+P4\+\_\+\+R\+O\+U\+T\+E(dest)\+:
\item called from \hyperlink{lwip_2src_2core_2ipv4_2ip_8c_a81facf31eb2f115e66227f648153ed79}{ip\+\_\+route()} (I\+Pv4)
\item dest\+: destination I\+Pv4 address Returns the destination netif or N\+U\+LL if no destination netif is found. In that case, \hyperlink{lwip_2src_2core_2ipv4_2ip_8c_a81facf31eb2f115e66227f648153ed79}{ip\+\_\+route()} continues as normal. L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL\+: After masking, the value of the debug is compared against this value. If it is smaller, then debugging messages are written. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ac095d0e53f5eb5b326b2cccfd071d93d}\label{opt_8h_ac095d0e53f5eb5b326b2cccfd071d93d}}

\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+S\+\_\+\+ON@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+D\+B\+G\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+S\+\_\+\+ON}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+H\+W\+A\+D\+D\+R\+H\+I\+NT}{LWIP\_NETIF\_HWADDRHINT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+H\+W\+A\+D\+D\+R\+H\+I\+NT~0}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+H\+W\+A\+D\+D\+R\+H\+I\+NT==1\+: \hyperlink{struct_cache}{Cache} link-\/layer-\/address hints (e.\+g. table indices) in struct netif. T\+CP and U\+DP can make use of this to prevent scanning the A\+RP table for every sent packet. While this is faster for big A\+RP tables or many concurrent connections, it might be counterproductive if you have a tiny A\+RP table or if there never are concurrent connections. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a1a446932dd927cc4136ba654c13bb97b}\label{opt_8h_a1a446932dd927cc4136ba654c13bb97b}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK}{LWIP\_NETIF\_LINK\_CALLBACK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK~0}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+K\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK==1\+: Support a callback function from an interface whenever the link changes (i.\+e., link down) \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a724a0ea765d5a47d026d529725f31c01}\label{opt_8h_a724a0ea765d5a47d026d529725f31c01}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+CK}{LWIP\_NETIF\_LOOPBACK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+CK~0}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+CK==1\+: Support sending packets with a destination IP address equal to the netif IP address, looping them back up the stack. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_aa28d13ddd5281b1912276991e7ea58c5}\label{opt_8h_aa28d13ddd5281b1912276991e7ea58c5}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG}}
\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG}{LWIP\_NETIF\_LOOPBACK\_MULTITHREADING}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG~(!\hyperlink{opt_8h_ae00ba99de94a5bf84d832be8976df59b}{N\+O\+\_\+\+S\+YS})}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG\+: Indicates whether threading is enabled in the system, as netifs must change how they behave depending on this setting for the L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+CK option to work. Setting this is needed to avoid reentering non-\/reentrant functions like tcp\+\_\+input(). L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG==1\+: Indicates that the user is using a multithreaded environment like \hyperlink{tcpip_8c}{tcpip.\+c}. In this case, netif-\/$>$input() is called directly. L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+L\+O\+O\+P\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+T\+H\+R\+E\+A\+D\+I\+NG==0\+: Indicates a polling (or N\+O\+\_\+\+S\+YS) setup. The packets are put on a list and netif\+\_\+poll() must be called in the main application loop. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9c942c2e9655b06d4f73c630d30f60bf}\label{opt_8h_a9c942c2e9655b06d4f73c630d30f60bf}}

\index{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK@{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK}{LWIP\_NETIF\_REMOVE\_CALLBACK}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK~0}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+B\+UF}{LWIP\_NETIF\_TX\_SINGLE\_PBUF}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+B\+UF~0}

L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+N\+E\+T\+I\+F\+\_\+\+T\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+B\+UF\+: if this is set to 1, lw\+IP tries to put all data to be sent into one single pbuf. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} is for compatibility with D\+M\+A-\/enabled M\+A\+Cs that do not support scatter-\/gather. Beware that this might involve C\+P\+U-\/memcpy before transmitting that would not be needed without this flag! Use this only if you need to!

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+LS}{MEM\_USE\_POOLS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+LS~0}

M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+LS==1\+: Use an alternative to malloc() by allocating from a set of memory pools of various sizes. When mem\+\_\+malloc is called, an element of the smallest pool that can provide the length needed is returned. To use this, M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+C\+U\+S\+T\+O\+M\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+LS also has to be enabled. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_aba8be68e8fd0716b723ce4569ed89f82}\label{opt_8h_aba8be68e8fd0716b723ce4569ed89f82}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL@{M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL}}
\index{M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL@{M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL}{MEM\_USE\_POOLS\_TRY\_BIGGER\_POOL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL~0}

M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+OL==1\+: if one malloc-\/pool is empty, try the next bigger pool -\/ W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG\+: T\+H\+IS M\+I\+G\+HT W\+A\+S\+TE M\+E\+M\+O\+RY but it can make a system more reliable. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_aa1dd57a66b6de8c0593e9e3e8d1411f6}\label{opt_8h_aa1dd57a66b6de8c0593e9e3e8d1411f6}}

M\+E\+M\+C\+PY\+: override this if you have a faster implementation at hand than the one included in your \hyperlink{struct_c}{C} library \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ad80231923f7a808d49eba5ec57d63616}\label{opt_8h_ad80231923f7a808d49eba5ec57d63616}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK}{MEMP\_OVERFLOW\_CHECK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK~0}

M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK\+: memp overflow protection reserves a configurable amount of bytes before and after each memp element in every pool and fills it with a prominent default value. M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK == 0 no checking M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK == 1 checks each element when it is freed M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK $>$= 2 checks each element in every pool every time \hyperlink{memp_8c_a2b00593d086313c267b54a976bf67aa5}{memp\+\_\+malloc()} or \hyperlink{memp_8c_aecd94926b7c2a0e23ae195f4ae97581f}{memp\+\_\+free()} is called (useful but slow!) \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a0838947193e222a9f46b582e01e5beff}\label{opt_8h_a0838947193e222a9f46b582e01e5beff}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+N\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK@{M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+N\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK}}
\index{M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+N\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK@{M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+N\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+N\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK~0}

M\+E\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+N\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+CK==1\+: run a sanity check after each \hyperlink{memp_8c_aecd94926b7c2a0e23ae195f4ae97581f}{memp\+\_\+free()} to make sure that there are no cycles in the linked lists. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a2e6aaf9504e7018db42014af3942187e}\label{opt_8h_a2e6aaf9504e7018db42014af3942187e}}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+C\+U\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+E\+F\+F\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+M\+SS\+: "The maximum size of a segment that T\+CP really sends, the \textquotesingle{}effective send M\+SS,\textquotesingle{} M\+U\+ST be the smaller of the send M\+SS (which reflects the available reassembly buffer size at the remote host) and the largest size permitted by the IP layer" (R\+FC 1122) Setting this to 1 enables code that checks T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS against the M\+TU of the netif used for a connection and limits the M\+SS if it would be too big otherwise. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a66df03d8192cd978d3321a9d68bf5411}\label{opt_8h_a66df03d8192cd978d3321a9d68bf5411}}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+R\+TX\+: Maximum number of retransmissions of data segments. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}\label{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS}{TCP\_MSS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS~536}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS\+: T\+CP Maximum segment size. (default is 536, a conservative default, you might want to increase this.) For the receive side, this M\+SS is advertised to the remote side when opening a connection. For the transmit size, this M\+SS sets an upper limit on the M\+SS advertised by the remote host. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9d6d3219bb5fc0bc760a64114de13c25}\label{opt_8h_a9d6d3219bb5fc0bc760a64114de13c25}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+O\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+ES~0}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+O\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+ES\+: The maximum number of bytes queued on ooseq per pcb. Default is 0 (no limit). T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG\+: Enable debugging in \hyperlink{tcp__out_8c}{tcp\+\_\+out.\+c} output functions. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a5648e2580bb55c0efdfbebcf3bad1eef}\label{opt_8h_a5648e2580bb55c0efdfbebcf3bad1eef}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE@{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE}}
\index{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE@{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE}{TCP\_OVERSIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE~\hyperlink{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS}}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ZE\+: The maximum number of bytes that tcp\+\_\+write may allocate ahead of time in an attempt to create shorter pbuf chains for transmission. The meaningful range is 0 to T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS. Some suggested values are\+:

0\+: Disable oversized allocation. Each tcp\+\_\+write() allocates a new pbuf (old behaviour). 1\+: Allocate size-\/aligned pbufs with minimal excess. Use this if your scatter-\/gather D\+MA requires aligned fragments. 128\+: Limit the pbuf/memory overhead to 20\%. T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS\+: Try to create unfragmented T\+CP packets. T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+S\+S/4\+: Try to create 4 fragments or less per T\+CP packet. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ae7980c7f8eb45cd411bf410ff0a3fc55}\label{opt_8h_ae7980c7f8eb45cd411bf410ff0a3fc55}} 
\index{opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}!T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+L\+E\+N\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG@{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+L\+E\+N\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG}}
\index{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+L\+E\+N\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG@{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+L\+E\+N\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+\_\+\+O\+O\+S\+EQ==1\+: T\+CP will queue segments that arrive out of order. Define to 0 if your device is low on memory. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a37596f7bbb9b7663826244ba54486679}\label{opt_8h_a37596f7bbb9b7663826244ba54486679}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+UF~(2 $\ast$ \hyperlink{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS})}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+UF\+: T\+CP sender buffer space (bytes). To achieve good performance, this should be at least 2 $\ast$ T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a9beaa47832ead4180981bfbf71074904}\label{opt_8h_a9beaa47832ead4180981bfbf71074904}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+EN}{TCP\_SND\_QUEUELEN}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+EN~((4 $\ast$ (\hyperlink{opt_8h_a871d111968d8c6c7880ff36b93c5c4dd}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+UF}) + (\hyperlink{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS} -\/ 1))/(\hyperlink{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS}))}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+EN\+: T\+CP sender buffer space (pbufs). \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} must be at least as much as (2 $\ast$ T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F/\+T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS) for things to work. \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_ae5c9866d7cd463ac7b36792182145aec}\label{opt_8h_ae5c9866d7cd463ac7b36792182145aec}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+L\+O\+W\+AT}{TCP\_SNDLOWAT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+L\+O\+W\+AT~L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+IN(L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AX(((\hyperlink{opt_8h_a871d111968d8c6c7880ff36b93c5c4dd}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+UF})/2), (2 $\ast$ \hyperlink{opt_8h_af1ab7bb27860aa3677c387a2f3ba317b}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+M\+SS}) + 1), (\hyperlink{opt_8h_a871d111968d8c6c7880ff36b93c5c4dd}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+UF}) -\/ 1)}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+L\+O\+W\+AT\+: T\+CP writable space (bytes). \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} must be less than T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+UF. \hyperlink{class_it}{It} is the amount of space which must be available in the T\+CP snd\+\_\+buf for select to return writable (combined with T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+O\+W\+AT). \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_a75659867592a6b01c198532ed1b65698}\label{opt_8h_a75659867592a6b01c198532ed1b65698}}

\index{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+O\+W\+AT@{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+O\+W\+AT}!opt.\+h@{opt.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+O\+W\+AT}{TCP\_SNDQUEUELOWAT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+O\+W\+AT~L\+W\+I\+P\+\_\+\+M\+AX(((\hyperlink{opt_8h_a9beaa47832ead4180981bfbf71074904}{T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+EN})/2), 5)}

T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+O\+W\+AT\+: T\+CP writable bufs (pbuf count). \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} must be less than T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+U\+E\+L\+EN. If the number of pbufs queued on a pcb drops below this number, select returns writable (combined with T\+C\+P\+\_\+\+S\+N\+D\+L\+O\+W\+AT). \mbox{\Hypertarget{opt_8h_aa02ec5c5bc0edebe418680c54d044f58}\label{opt_8h_aa02ec5c5bc0edebe418680c54d044f58}}
